253→function areSame(localContent: string, remoteContent: string, ignoredSettings: string[]): boolean {\n   254→\tif (localContent === remoteContent) {\n   255→\t\treturn true;\n   256→\t}\n   257→\n   258→\tconst local = parse(localContent);\n   259→\tconst remote = parse(remoteContent);\n   260→\tconst ignored = ignoredSettings.reduce((set, key) => { set.add(key); return set; }, new   294→\t}\n   295→\treturn true;\n   296→}\n   297→\n   298→function compare(from: IStringDictionary<any> | null, to: IStringDictionary<any>, ignored: Set<string>): { added: Set<string>; removed: Set<string>; updated: Set<string> } {\n   299→\tconst fromKeys = from ? 253→function areSame(localContent: string, remoteContent: string, ignoredSettings: string[]): boolean {\n   254→\tif (localContent === remoteContent) {\n   255→\t\treturn true;\n   256→\t}\n   257→\n   294→\t}\n   295→\treturn true;\n   296→}\n   297→\n   298→function compare(from: IStringDictionary<any> | null, to: IStringDictionary<any>, ignored: Set<string>): { added: Set<string>; removed:
